<Review>Ahhh yes. How can one "not" enjoy the flavorful establishment that has now become a legendary staple in the city of Bakersfield, California. Just Wing It provides a plethora of tasty delicacy that needn't be, dare I say, just wings. The Cheesy Bacon Burger is a personal favorite that is cooked to taste, and is perfected everytime. The chipotle mayo spread across the bun is a a slight spice of delight. But if it's wings you're looking for, than you've stepped into the right place. Whether you're looking for traditional wings, super spicy wings (Dead Man Walking) or simple flavors (Garlic Parmasean, Lemon Pepper) this is the right place. Do you like bacon? Because you can get your wings bacon wrapped!  Customer service is amazing here! As a returning customer, I don't ever need to ask for a beer or food. The amazing employees know what I like everytime I come in to their establishment. It's almost like walking into an episode of the hit 80's television show, "Cheers". It truly is a place where everybody knows your name.  If you need a place for great food and great customer service, Just Wing It is the place to go. Bring the family, bring the friends and come enjoy great food and a great environment.< /Review>< pictures>

<Name>Alexander Goldshmidt< /Name><Review>Decent if you are stuck at the middle of the road  at 12 PM<//Review><rating>3<//rating><time>1536503230949</time>< gmapID>

<text>First of all I have to say I am VERY impressed with the manager, Tom. I called in a To-Go order on a busy Sun. morning, when I called back later to say "Thank you" Tom recognized my voice & even remembered my name! He was very upbeat & made it a JOY to order from him :) (Also kudos to him because I assume he was manning the front because they were down a staff member, & doing a great job!). I ordered my eggs over-medium & bacon crispy, I was worried my egg whites might still be slimy & I'd have to re-cook the bacon also. But not at all! The eggs were soo perfect, exactly what I wanted & the bacon too! Oh & the oatmeal is perfect (I like it more runny than thick). I'm pregnant & was really craving this, so I could not be more happy right now :)) Previously I chose to stay the heck away from Denny's (for about 8 yrs!) due to several negative experiences years ago at a diff. location, I won't say exactly what the last straw was because it's gross, but basically there was something in my food that shouldn't have been there :( So you can imagine my apprehensiveness about eating at any Denny's. Since visiting this location 3-4 times my trust in Denny's (at least this location) is fully restored! Every time we go the servers are upbeat & polite making it an enjoyable dining experience, & I've been pretty impressed with the food being cooked to order as well. Lastly it's a nice atmosphere, I don't know if they re-did it or maybe there was a steakhouse there previously & they kept the design/ deco., but it's a very nice setting as well.
